As a consequence, all foods containing animal fat contain cholesterol to varying extents. Major dietary sources of cholesterol include cheese, egg yolks, beef, pork, poultry, fish, and shrimp. Human breast milk also contains significant quantities of cholesterol.\r\n\r\nFrom a dietary perspective, cholesterol is not found in significant amounts in plant sources.
